<p><img src="http://archive.org/download/RubenerdShow238/RubenerdShow238.png" alt="Do I look like I'm thinking?" style="height:240px; width:240px; float:right; margin:0 0 10px 20px;" /></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold">The why I am an atheist episode.</p>

<p>A bit more serious: discussing the reasons why I became an atheist from experiences in my early childhood to the present, including most recently my beautiful mummy&#39;s struggle with cancer and passing on.</p>

<p>Also briefly refuting some of the misconceptions about atheists including intolerance, arrogance, spirituality, materialism, wishful thinking, heaven, the celestial dictatorship, and why <a href="http://twitter.com/ons/statuses/785717461">statements like this</a> are completely untrue.</p>

<p><strong>BONUS:</strong> A very quick, foolproof test you can use to see if someone who trashes evolution has actually studied it.</p>

<p><strong>DISCLAIMER:</strong> This episode was not recorded to insult people, it&#39;s just an explanation for why personally I&#39;m atheist. If you are religious you may be offended, but please know that in my heart that it was not my intention.</p>

<div style="text-align:center"><em>You may say I'm a dreamer
But I'm not the only one
I hope someday you'll join us
And the world will be as one.</em></div>
